# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

Perfect! I've successfully completed the analysis of Apache Kafka's consumer offset management architecture and created a comprehensive `answer.json` file. Here's a summary of my findings:

## Key Components Found

### **Core Storage & Management**
1. **OffsetMetadataManager** - The central component managing all offset operations:
   - Stores offsets in memory (Timeline HashMap)
   - Handles offset commits, fetches, deletes
   - Implements cleanup of expired offsets
   - Generates tombstone records for log compaction

2. **OffsetAndMetadata** - Dual implementations:
   - Server-side: Stores committed offset, leader epoch, metadata, timestamps, topic ID
   - Client-side: Used by consumers for offset tracking

### **Request Handlers**
3. **KafkaApis.scala** - The request processor layer:
   - `handleOffsetCommitRequest` - Processes offset commit requests
   - `handleOffsetFetchRequest` - Processes offset fetch requests

4. **GroupCoordinator Interface** with implementations:
   - **GroupCoordinatorService** - High-level service
   - **GroupCoordinatorShard** - Replicated state machine handling requests

### **Expiry & Compaction Logic**
5. **OffsetExpirationCondition** interface & **OffsetExpirationConditionImpl**:
   - Determines when offsets expire based on retention period (default 7 days)
   - **cleanupExpiredOffsets** method removes stale offsets

6. **Log Compaction Integration**:
   - Tombstone records (null values) mark deleted offsets
   - Log cleaner removes old offset entries from __consumer_offsets topic
   - Maintains only latest offset for each group-topic-partition

### **Supporting Components**
- **GroupMetadataManager** - Tracks group lifecycle and offset expiration conditions
- **GroupCoordinatorConfig** - Configures offset retention and storage setting

(`group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupCoordinatorService.java`) - High-level coordinator service that delegates to shard\\n- **GroupCoordinatorShard** (`group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupCoordinatorShard.java`) - Replicated state machine handling offset commit/fetch for a specific partition\\n\\n#### Offset Commit Handler\\nThe commit flow:\\n1. **handleOffsetCommitRequest** in `KafkaApis.scala` - Receives OffsetCommitRequest from client\\n2. Routes to **GroupCoordinator.handleOffsetCommit** via GroupCoordinatorService\\n3. **GroupCoordinatorShard.handleOffsetCommit** - Processes and generates CoordinatorRecords\\n4. **OffsetMetadataManager.handleCommitOffsets** - Stores offset in memory and generates write records\\n\\n#### OffsetFetch Request Processor\\nThe fetch flow:\\n1. **handleOffsetFetchRequest** in `KafkaApis.scala` - Receives OffsetFetchRequest\\n2. Routes to **GroupCoordinator.fetchOffsets** via GroupCoordinatorService\\n3. **GroupCoordinatorShard.handleOffsetFetch** - Validates authorization\\n4. **OffsetMetadataManager.fetchOffsets** - Retrieves offsets from memory\\n\\n### OffsetMetadataManager - Core Offset Storage\\n\\nThe `OffsetMetadataManager` (`group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/OffsetMetadataManager.java`) manages:\\n- **offsets** - Timeline HashMap storing group -> topic -> partition -> OffsetAndMetadata\\n- **pendingTransactionalOffsets** - Tracks transactional offsets not yet committed\\n- **openTransactions** - Tracks groups with ongoing transactions\\n\\nKey methods:\\n- **handleCommitOffsets** - Handles offset commit requests and generates tombstone records for replacements\\n- **fetchOffsets** - Retrieves committed offsets for fetch requests\\n- **deleteOffsets** - Deletes offsets (OffsetDelete API)\\n- **onPartitionsDeleted** - Cleans up offsets when topics are deleted\\n- **cleanupExpiredOffsets** - Removes expired offsets\\n\\n### Offset Expiry and Compaction Logic\\n\\n**OffsetExpirationCondition** interface (`group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/OffsetExpirationCondition.java`) defines when an offset expires:\\n\\n**OffsetExpirationConditionImpl** (`group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/OffsetExpirationConditionImpl.java`) implements expiration based on:\\n- Base timestamp (commit timestamp for consumer offsets)\\n- Configured retention period (offsets.retention.minutes)\\n- Current time\\n\\n**Offset cleanup** in `OffsetMetadataManager.cleanupExpiredOffsets`:\\n- Iterates through all offsets for groups not subscribed to topics\\n- Checks if offset has expired using OffsetExpirationCondition\\n- Appends tombstone records (null values) for expired offsets\\n- Tombstone records enable log compaction to remove old entries\\n- Records cleanup metric via OFFSET_EXPIRED_SENSOR_NAME\\n\\n**Log Compaction**: The __consumer_offsets topic uses log compaction (cleanup.policy=compact):\\n- Tombstone records (null values) mark deleted offsets\\n- Log cleaner removes entries with identical keys and null values\\n- Maintains only the latest offset for each group-topic-partition\\n\\n### Group Metadata Management\\n\\nThe `GroupMetadataManager` (`group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupMetadataManager.java`) tracks:\\n- Group lifecycle and state\\n- Which groups have active offsets\\n- Group expiration conditions\\n\\nDifferent group types support different offset expiration:\\n- **ClassicGroup** - Expires based on last commit timestamp\\n- **ConsumerGroup** - Expires based on last commit timestamp  \\n- **StreamsGroup** - Expires based on last commit timestamp\\n- **ShareGroup** - Does not support offset expiration\\n\\n### Request/Response Protocol\\n\\nThe offset management uses these protocol requests/responses:\\n- **OffsetCommitRequest/Response** - Commits offsets for a consumer group\\n- **OffsetFetchRequest/Response** - Fetches committed offsets\\n- **OffsetDeleteRequest/Response** - Deletes offsets (Admin API)\\n\\nProtocol definitions automatically generate key/value classes for __consumer_offsets records.\\n\\n### Configuration\\n\\n`GroupCoordinatorConfig` defines critical offset settings:\\n- offsetsRetentionMs - How long to keep offsets (default 7 days)\\n- offsetMetadataMaxSize - Maximum metadata size per offset\\n- offsetsTopicPartitions - Number of partitions in __consumer_offsets\\n- offsetsTopicReplicationFactor - Replication factor for offset storage\\n\\nThis architecture ensures durable, scalable offset management with automatic cleanup and compaction of the __consumer_offsets topic.\"\n}\n",

Routes to **GroupCoordinator.handleOffsetCommit** via GroupCoordinatorService\\n3. **GroupCoordinatorShard.handleOffsetCommit** - Processes and generates CoordinatorRecords\\n4. **OffsetMetadataManager.handleCommitOffsets** - Stores offset in memory and generates write records\\n\\n#### OffsetFetch Request Processor\\nThe fetch flow:\\n1. **handleOffsetFetchRequest** in `KafkaApis.scala` - Receives OffsetFetchRequest\\n2. Routes to **GroupCoordinator.fetchOffsets** via GroupCoordinatorService\\n3. **GroupCoordinatorShard.handleOffsetFetch** - Validates authorization\\n4. **OffsetMetadataManager.fetchOffsets** - Retrieves offsets from memory\\n\\n### OffsetMetadataManager - Core Offset Storage\\n\\nThe `OffsetMetadataManager` (`group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/OffsetMetadataManager.java`) manages:\\n- **offsets** - Timeline HashMap storing group -> topic -> partition -> OffsetAndMetadata\\n- **pendingTransactionalOffsets** - Tracks transactional offsets not yet committed\\n- **openTransactions** - Tracks groups with ongoing transactions\\n\\nKey methods:\\n- **handleCommitOffsets** - Handles offset commit requests and generates tombstone records for replacements\\n- **fetchOffsets** - Retrieves committed offsets for fetch requests\\n- **deleteOffsets** - Deletes offsets (OffsetDelete API)\\n- **onPartitionsDeleted** - Cleans up offsets when topics are deleted\\n- **cleanupExpiredOffsets** - Expires based on last commit timestamp\\n- **ConsumerGroup** - Expires based on last commit timestamp  \\n- **StreamsGroup** - Expires based on last commit timestamp\\n- **ShareGroup** - Does not support offset expiration\\n\\n### Request/Response Protocol\\n\\nThe offset management uses these protocol requests/responses:\\n- **OffsetCommitRequest/Response** - Commits offsets for a consumer group\\n- **OffsetFetchRequest/Response** - Fetches committed offsets\\n- **OffsetDeleteRequest/Response** - Deletes offsets (Admin API)\\n\\nProtocol definitions automatically generate key/value classes for __consumer_offsets records.\\n\\n### Configuration\\n\\n`GroupCoordinatorConfig` defines critical offset settings:\\n- offsetsRetentionMs - How long to keep offsets (default 7 days)\\n- offsetMetadataMaxSize - Maximum metadata size per offset\\n- offsetsTopicPartitions - Number of partitions in __consumer_offsets\\n- offsetsTopicReplicationFactor - Replication factor for offset storage\\n\\nThis architecture ensures durable, scalable offset management with automatic cleanup and compaction of the __consumer_offsets topic.\"\n}\n",
